CREATE DATABASE IF NOT EXISTS CONSTRUCTION_SAAS;
USE DATABASE CONSTRUCTION_SAAS;

CREATE SCHEMA IF NOT EXISTS CORTEX_AI;
USE SCHEMA CORTEX_AI;

-- ══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
-- FACT_SUPPORT_TICKET — 1000 rows
-- DIM_CUSTOMER: 100 customers (IDs 1–100)
-- DIM_PRODUCT:  5 products  (IDs 1–5)
-- ══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════

-- ── DIM_PRODUCT ──────────────────────────────────────────────────
CREATE OR REPLACE TABLE DIM_PRODUCT (
    PRODUCT_ID        NUMBER        NOT NULL PRIMARY KEY,
    PRODUCT_NAME      VARCHAR(100)  NOT NULL,
    PRODUCT_CATEGORY  VARCHAR(100),
    PLAN_TIER         VARCHAR(50)
);

INSERT INTO DIM_PRODUCT VALUES
    (1, 'CrewPay',       'Payroll & Compliance',         'Enterprise'),
    (2, 'CrewScheduler', 'Workforce Scheduling',          'Enterprise'),
    (3, 'FieldForce',    'Field Worker Mobile App',       'Standard'),
    (4, 'BidBuilder',    'Project Estimating & Bidding',  'Enterprise'),
    (5, 'OnboardIQ',     'HR & Document Management',      'Standard');

-- ── DIM_CUSTOMER (100 customers) ─────────────────────────────────
CREATE OR REPLACE TABLE DIM_CUSTOMER (
    CUSTOMER_ID    NUMBER       NOT NULL PRIMARY KEY,
    COMPANY_NAME   VARCHAR(150) NOT NULL,
    PROVINCE       VARCHAR(5),
    COMPANY_SIZE   VARCHAR(50),
    SUPPORT_TIER   VARCHAR(50),
    CUSTOMER_SINCE DATE
);

-- ── FACT_SUPPORT_TICKET ──────────────────────────────────────────
CREATE OR REPLACE TABLE FACT_SUPPORT_TICKET (
    TICKET_ID    NUMBER        NOT NULL PRIMARY KEY,
    CUSTOMER_ID  NUMBER        NOT NULL REFERENCES DIM_CUSTOMER(CUSTOMER_ID),
    PRODUCT_ID   NUMBER        NOT NULL REFERENCES DIM_PRODUCT(PRODUCT_ID),
    PRIORITY     VARCHAR(20),
    STATUS       VARCHAR(30),
    CHANNEL      VARCHAR(30),
    TICKET_TEXT  VARCHAR(4000),
    CREATED_AT   TIMESTAMP_NTZ,
    RESOLVED_AT  TIMESTAMP_NTZ
);
